## Interaction Log

### System — 2026-07-01T23:01:26.141189

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Perform a full operational health check of the OWL swarm stack.

**Required actions:**
1. Call `blofin_get_stack_health` (no parameters) to obtain operational health snapshot (caches, feeds, errors, equity).
2. Call `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` (no parameters) to retrieve the latest swarm learning report (what was learned, improved, fixed, with proof).
3. Combine the two results into a **strict JSON** object with the following keys:
   - `status`: overall health status (e.g., "healthy", "degraded", "critical").
   - `issues`: list of identified problems or anomalies from both sources.
   - `repair_actions`: recommended remediation steps for each issue.
   - `confidence`: numeric confidence (0‑1) in the assessment.
   - `narrative`: concise human‑readable summary explaining the findings and rationale.

**Constraints:**
- Output must be valid JSON adhering exactly to the schema above.
- No additional text or formatting outside the JSON object.

**Context:** The agent has access to a large toolbox of Blofin functions (portfolio assessment, positions, equity, trade insights, tactics research, TP/SL management, ranking opportunities, news, funding rates, ticker, universe snapshot, position sizing, technical analysis, order execution, instrument specs, order placement/cancellation, candles, order book, stack health, swarm learning report, self‑heal playbook, pentest utilities, handoff delegation, instrument list). For this request only `blofin_get_stack_health` and `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` are needed.
